***ontvangen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ontvangen.html>ontvangen</a> (1515)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ontvaan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ontvaen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">antfān</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ont-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vangen.html>vangen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ontvangen.html>ontvangen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to receive
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Irène Joliot-Curie <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ontving.html>ontving</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:samen.html>samen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> Frédéric Joliot <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> Nobelprijs <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:scheikunde.html>Scheikunde</a>, in 1935, <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jaar.html>jaar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:overlijden.html>overlijden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moeder.html>moeder</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Irène Joliot-Curie <b>received</b>, together with her husband Frédéric Joliot, a Nobel Prize for Chemistry in 1935, one year after the death of her mother.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
